country_event = { #Berlin stock crisis
	id = netherlands_starting_events.2
	title = netherlands_starting_events.2.t
	desc = netherlands_starting_events.2.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_black_monday

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { add_ideas = HOL_idea_crisis }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_starting_events.2 option netherlands_starting_events.2.a"
		name = netherlands_starting_events.2.a
		add_stability = -0.25
		effect_tooltip = { add_ideas = HOL_idea_crisis }
	}
}

		add_ideas = HOL_idea_instability

		}
	}
}

		name = netherlands_starting_events.4.a

			ideology = social_democrat
			name = HOL_election_social_democrat_party

		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			name = HOL_election_social_liberal_party
			long_name = HOL_election_social_liberal_party_long
		}
	}
}

###################################
# Dutch Elections 1937

country_event = { #Dutch Elections 1937
	id = netherlands_election_events.1
	title = netherlands_election_events.1.t
	desc = netherlands_election_events.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_election_1937

	trigger = {
		date < 1938.01.01
		has_elected_government = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				name = HOL_social_democrat_party
				long_name = HOL_social_democrat_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				name = HOL_social_liberal_party
				long_name = HOL_social_liberal_party_long
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.1 option netherlands_election_events.1.a"
		name = netherlands_election_events.1.a #Lijst Links wins a majority
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		HOL_albarda_sic = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_left_list_victorious
		country_event = { id = netherlands_election_events.2 days = 3 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				5 = {
					GER = { country_event = { id = netherlands_election_events.7 hours = 8 } } #Reijnders requests support from Germany
				}
				95 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_AUTDEM }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.1 option netherlands_election_events.1.b"
		name = netherlands_election_events.1.b #CNA narrowly wins a majority
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.01
		}
		HOL_colijn_sic = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_CNA_gamble_worked
		country_event = { id = netherlands_election_events.3 days = 3 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.1 option netherlands_election_events.1.c"
		name = netherlands_election_events.1.c #CNA is overtaken by the VNH from the right;
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NAS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_KAPN_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_RSAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_SDAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		HOL_swart_sic = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_VNH_victory
		country_event = { id = netherlands_election_events.4 days = 3 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Lijst Links victorious, but Wilhelmina will only accept a left government with VDB PM
	id = netherlands_election_events.2
	title = netherlands_election_events.2.t
	desc = netherlands_election_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_SDAP_victory_37

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.2 option netherlands_election_events.2.a"
		name = netherlands_election_events.2.a #SDAP and VDB form government, wilhelminas demand accepted
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NAS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_KAPN_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_RSAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_SDAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		HOL_oud_sic = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_VDB_SDAP
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.2 option netherlands_election_events.2.b"
		name = netherlands_election_events.2.b #SDAP won the elections, works with RSAP in defiance of Wilhelmina
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_MARLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_SDAP_RSAP
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = netherlands_election_events.6 days = 3 } #Wilhelmina abdicates
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			news_event = netherlands_flavour_events.20
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #CNA victorious - get a coalition partner?
	id = netherlands_election_events.3
	title = netherlands_election_events.3.t
	desc = netherlands_election_events.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_cna_victory_37

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.3 option netherlands_election_events.3.a"
		name = netherlands_election_events.3.a #Add the market liberals to cabinet
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_work_with_LSP
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.3 option netherlands_election_events.3.b"
		name = netherlands_election_events.3.b #CNA rules on its own
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = HOL_CNA_on_its_own
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.3 option netherlands_election_events.3.c"
		name = netherlands_election_events.3.c #Add the VNH to cabinet
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_alliance_of_the_right
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			news_event = netherlands_flavour_events.20
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #VNH victorious - what now?
	id = netherlands_election_events.4
	title = netherlands_election_events.4.t
	desc = netherlands_election_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_vnh_poster

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.4 option netherlands_election_events.4.a"
		name = netherlands_election_events.4.a #Form cabinet with CNA
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = { date < 1939.1.1 }
			complete_national_focus = HOL_alliance_of_the_right
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = netherlands_flavour_events.20
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.4 option netherlands_election_events.4.b"
		name = netherlands_election_events.4.b #Let landwacht intimidate second chamber into giving emergency powers to VNH
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = { date < 1939.1.1 }
			complete_national_focus = HOL_intimidate_parliament
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = netherlands_flavour_events.23
		}
	}
}

		set_politics = {

		}
		HOL_revolution_effect = yes

	}
}

country_event = { #Wilhelmina's abdication (socdems)
	id = netherlands_election_events.6
	title = netherlands_election_events.6.t
	desc = netherlands_election_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_wilhelmina_abdication

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { character = HOL_wilhelmina_van_orange_nassau }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.6 option netherlands_election_events.6.a"
		name = netherlands_election_events.6.a #Declare the republic!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCDEM }
			}
		}
		HOL_remove_monarchy = yes
		HOL_parliament_sic = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.6 option netherlands_election_events.6.b"
		name = netherlands_election_events.6.b #Juliana shall be the next queen
		ai_chance = { base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_REP_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		retire_character = HOL_wilhelmina_van_orange_nassau
		HOL_create_juliana = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HOL_wilhelmina_van_orange_nassau = { kill_character = yes } #well, she's *politically* dead
			news_event = netherlands_flavour_events.26
		}
	}
}

			}

	}

country_event = { #Putsch succeeded, what now?
	id = netherlands_election_events.10
	title = netherlands_election_events.10.t
	desc = netherlands_election_events.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_putsch_succeeded

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.10 option netherlands_election_events.10.a"
		name = netherlands_election_events.10.a #Form junta
		ai_chance = { base = 70 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}
			clear_all_relations = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		HOL_reijnders_sic = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_junta_consolidation
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_election_events.10 option netherlands_election_events.10.b"
		name = netherlands_election_events.10.b #Install VNH as 'provisional government'
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}
			clear_all_relations = yes
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		HOL_swart_sic = yes
		complete_national_focus = HOL_intimidate_parliament
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = netherlands_flavour_events.21
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
				GER = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = netherlands_focus_events.69 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Torching of the binnenhof
	id = netherlands_post_election_events.1
	title = netherlands_post_election_events.1.t
	desc = netherlands_post_election_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_binnenhof_fire

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_authoritarian_government = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = hol_dont_burn_binnenhof
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep calm and carry on
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.1 option netherlands_post_election_events.1.a"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dictatorship_government = no }
				country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.2 days = 2 } #Antisyndicalist riots
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.86 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #declare state of emergency
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.1 option netherlands_post_election_events.1.b"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NAS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_KAPN_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_RSAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_SDAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NATPOP }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_authoritarian_government = no
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		HOL_reijnders_sic = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HOL_idea_negotiate_with_extremists }
			remove_ideas = HOL_idea_negotiate_with_extremists
		}
		complete_national_focus = HOL_reijnders_putsch
		complete_national_focus = HOL_junta_consolidation
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.2 days = 2 } #Antisyndicalist riots
		}
	}

	after = {
		set_country_flag = hol_binnenhof_burning
	}
}

				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Amerikavrijwilligers"

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Amerikavrijwilligers" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Amerikavrijwilligers" disband = yes } #no cheating
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Amerikavrijwilligers"
				division_names_group = USA_GAR_01

					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 358 360 }
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_spawn_unit
					TYPE = "Amerikavrijwilligers"
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Amerikavrijwilligers\" division_template = \"Amerikavrijwilligers\" start_experience_factor = 0"

					id = 1776
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Elections 1941 - Cabinet Colijn V sat out the ride
	id = netherlands_post_election_events.76
	title = netherlands_post_election_events.76.t
	desc = netherlands_post_election_events.76.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_election_1937

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1938.1.1
		date < 1942.1.1
		has_government = social_conservative
		is_monarchy = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = hol_lsp_to_the_left }
				}
				set_country_flag = hol_lsp_to_the_left
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.76 option netherlands_post_election_events.76.a"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.76.a #CNA attains again an absolute majority
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = HOL_stable_once_again
				has_completed_focus = HOL_democratic_survival
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.77 days = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.76 option netherlands_post_election_events.76.b"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.76.b #CNA gets the most seats but not '37s absolute majority
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
							has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
						}
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = HOL_stable_once_again
							has_completed_focus = HOL_democratic_survival
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.78 days = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.76 option netherlands_post_election_events.76.c"

			}

			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.78 option netherlands_post_election_events.78.c"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.78.c #CNA rules with the VNH

country_event = { #Elections [GetYear] another loop
	id = netherlands_post_election_events.111
	title = netherlands_post_election_events.111.t
	desc = netherlands_post_election_events.111.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1942.1.1
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_completed_focus = HOL_CNA_gamble_worked
		is_monarchy = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = hol_lsp_to_the_left }
				}
				set_country_flag = hol_lsp_to_the_left
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.111 option netherlands_post_election_events.111.a"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.111.a #CNA attains an absolute majority
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = HOL_stable_once_again
				has_completed_focus = HOL_democratic_survival
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		HOL_colijn_sic = yes
		country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.112 days = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.111 option netherlands_post_election_events.111.b"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.111.b #CNA gets the most seats but not '37s absolute majority
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
							has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
						}
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = HOL_stable_once_again
							has_completed_focus = HOL_democratic_survival
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		HOL_colijn_sic = yes
		country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.113 days = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.111 option netherlands_post_election_events.111.c"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.111.c #Progressive run to LSP - LSP sweeps elections
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = hol_lsp_to_the_left
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		HOL_schermerhorn_sic = yes
		country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.114 days = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.111 option netherlands_post_election_events.111.e"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.111.e #SDAP becomes the largest
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCCON_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_MON_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = HOL_red_scare }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		HOL_drees_sic = yes
		country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.115 days = 3 }
	}

country_event = { #The Batavian Commune forms and we need to react
	id = netherlands_post_election_events.117
	title = netherlands_post_election_events.117.t
	desc = netherlands_post_election_events.117.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_military_putsch_for_GER

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		can_declare_war_on = HOL
		HOL = {
			is_subject = no
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.117 option netherlands_post_election_events.117.a"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.117.a #Send agents to destabilise their regime
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NAS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_KAPN_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_RSAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_SDAP_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		add_manpower = -500
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -500
		}
		HOL = { country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.119 days = 1 } } #Germany messes with our politics
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.117 option netherlands_post_election_events.117.b"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.117.b #Invade the Commune and end it for once and for all
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = { #Don't screw over a Dutch player
				factor = 0
				HOL = { is_ai = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_war_with = FRA
				FRA = { surrender_progress < 0.25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				date < 1939.1.1
				OR = {
					HOL = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
					HOL = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
					HOL = { has_decision = hol_join_internationale_decision }
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = wk2_begin_options option = RARE }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				date < 1939.1.1
				OR = {
					HOL = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
					HOL = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
					HOL = { has_decision = hol_join_internationale_decision }
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = wk2_begin_options option = RESTRICTED }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_NAS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_KAPN_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_RSAP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = HOL_path option = HOL_PATH_SDAP_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = HOL
			type = annex_everything
		}
		HOL = { country_event = { id = netherlands_post_election_events.118 days = 1 } } #German invasion
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_stability = -0.05
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_post_election_events.117 option netherlands_post_election_events.117.c"
		name = netherlands_post_election_events.117.c #There is nothing we can do
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HOL_tt_do_nothing
	}
}

country_event = { #Trade Missions
	id = netherlands_focus_events.19
	title = netherlands_focus_events.19.t
	desc = netherlands_focus_events.19.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #To Scandinavia
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.19 option netherlands_focus_events.19.a"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.19.a
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				DEN = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				SWE = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				NOR = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				FIN = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = DEN
					tag = SWE
					tag = NOR
					tag = FIN
				}
				has_war = no
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
			country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.20 days = 67 } #two months preparation and week traveltime
		}
	}

	option = { #To North America
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.19 option netherlands_focus_events.19.b"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.19.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				CAN = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				var:361.owner = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				ACC = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				NEE = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				CUB = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAN
					tag = CUB
					is_american_tag = yes
				}
				has_war = no
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
			country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.20 days = 67 } #two months preparation and week traveltime
		}
	}

	option = { #To South America
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.19 option netherlands_focus_events.19.c"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.19.c
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				COL = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				VEN = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				BRA = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				ARG = {
					exists = yes
					has_war = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {

				OR = {
					tag = COL

					tag = BRA
					tag = ARG
				}
				has_war = no

	id = netherlands_focus_events.21
	title = netherlands_focus_events.21.t
	desc = netherlands_focus_events.21.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.21 option netherlands_focus_events.21.a"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.21.a
		set_country_flag = hol_trade_mission_back
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = { has_country_flag = HOL_accepted_trade_mission }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_accepted_trade_mission }
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = FROM
						modifier = KR_trade_agreement
					}
					reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = FROM
						modifier = KR_trade_agreement
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = hol_they_didnt_break_trade_barriers
			set_country_flag = hol_failed_trade_mission
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Negotiations with the left succeeded
	id = netherlands_focus_events.34
	title = netherlands_focus_events.34.t
	desc = netherlands_focus_events.34.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.34 option netherlands_focus_events.34.a"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.34.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_working_hours_2
					has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_working_hours_1
				}
			}
			add_ideas = HOL_idea_agreement_with_left_0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_working_hours_2 }
			add_ideas = HOL_idea_agreement_with_left_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_working_hours_1 }
			add_ideas = HOL_idea_agreement_with_left_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_recognition_1
					has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_recognition_2
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.41 days = 40 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_protection_2 }
			add_manpower = -4000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_protection_1 }
			add_manpower = -2000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_rnf_limits_2 }
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_rnf_limits_1 }
			add_stability = 0.02
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_nas_limits_2 }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_nas_limits_1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					syndicalist > 0.1
					syndicalist < 0.2
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					syndicalist > 0.2
					syndicalist < 0.3
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.3 }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.3
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_rsap_limits_2 }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hol_negotiations_rsap_limits_1 }
			if = {
				limit = { radical_socialist < 0.1 }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					popularity = -0.05
				}

					radical_socialist < 0.4
				}

				}

			if = {

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		HOL_oud_sic = yes
		country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.56 days = 3 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.55 option netherlands_focus_events.55.b"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.55.b #CNA loses their majority but remains the largest
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		HOL_colijn_sic = yes
		country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.57 days = 3 }
	}
}

		has_socialist_government = yes

		add_popularity = {

			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly } }
			complete_national_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly
		}
		complete_national_focus = HOL_one_raadspensionaris
	}
}

		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = hol_sdap_syndielegalized
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly } }
			complete_national_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					name = HOL_social_democrat_party
					long_name = HOL_social_democrat_party_long
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes
				promote_character = HOL_willem_drees
				complete_national_focus = HOL_social_democracy
			}
			50 = {
				promote_character = HOL_henk_sneevliet
				complete_national_focus = HOL_socialist_republic
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Compromise between the RSAP and NAS
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.66 option netherlands_focus_events.66.b"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.66.b
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly } }
			complete_national_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = syndicalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				complete_national_focus = HOL_vakbondsfederatie
			}
			50 = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				complete_national_focus = HOL_socialist_republic
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Paul de Groot coups the government with the RNF
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.66 option netherlands_focus_events.66.c"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.66.c
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			name = HOL_event_rnf
			long_name = HOL_event_rnf_long
		}
		promote_character = HOL_paul_de_groot
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly } }
			complete_national_focus = HOL_third_national_assembly
		}
		complete_national_focus = HOL_one_raadspensionaris
	}
}

	desc = netherlands_focus_events.75.d

		original_tag = AST
		JAP = {
			has_war_with = HOL
			is_subject = no
		}
		is_in_faction_with = ENT
		is_subject = no
		HOL = {
			is_in_faction = no
			is_subject = no
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = ENT }
			all_enemy_country = {
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = JAP
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Let's do it!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.75 option netherlands_focus_events.75.a"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.75.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = no }
			faction_leader = { country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.77 days = 1 } }
		}
		else = {
			HOL = { country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.76 days = 3 } }
		}
	}

	option = { #No, it doesn't seem worth it
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.75 option netherlands_focus_events.75.b"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.75.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Policy on Belgium
	id = netherlands_focus_events.86
	title = netherlands_focus_events.86.t
	desc = netherlands_focus_events.86.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Every Dutchman in one country!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.86 option netherlands_focus_events.86.a"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.86.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_democratic_government = no
				NOT = {
					country_exists = BEL
					country_exists = FLA
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = social_democrat
						has_socialist_government = yes
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							country_exists = BEL
							BEL = {
								has_socialist_government = yes
							}
						}
						AND = {
							country_exists = FLA
							FLA = {
								has_socialist_government = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		add_state_claim = 6
		add_state_claim = 29
		add_state_claim = 925
	}

	option = { #Belgo-Dutch Friendship is mutually beneficial
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.86 option netherlands_focus_events.86.b"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.86.b
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = BEL
				country_exists = FLA
			}
			NOT = { #If you're socialist and we're not then you're beyond saving
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = social_democrat
						has_government = radical_socialist
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = totalist
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							country_exists = BEL
							BEL = {
								has_socialist_government = yes
							}
						}
						AND = {
							country_exists = FLA
							FLA = {
								has_socialist_government = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = hol_friendship_with_belgium
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = BEL }
			BEL = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = HOL
					modifier = HOL_belgodutch_friendship
				}
			}
			HOL = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = BEL
					modifier = HOL_belgodutch_friendship
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = FLA }
			FLA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = HOL
					modifier = HOL_belgodutch_friendship
				}
			}
			HOL = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = FLA
					modifier = HOL_belgodutch_friendship
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				factor = 2
				surrender_progress > 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				surrender_progress > 0.4
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				surrender_progress > 0.6
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				surrender_progress > 0.8
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_belgian_tag = yes
				is_in_faction = no
				FROM = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { var:6.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				6 = { transfer_state_to = FROM }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:29.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				29 = { transfer_state_to = FROM }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:925.owner = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
				925 = { transfer_state_to = FROM }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.88 days = 2 } }

			base = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				surrender_progress > 0.6
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = netherlands_focus_events.89 days = 2 } }
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Abandon the Boers
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_focus_events.91 option netherlands_focus_events.91.b"
		name = netherlands_focus_events.91.b
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_democratic_government = yes
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #First VNH Landdag since seizing power
	id = netherlands_flavour_events.11
	title = netherlands_flavour_events.11.t
	desc = netherlands_flavour_events.11.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1937.09.01
				date < 1937.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1938.09.01
				date < 1938.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1939.09.01
				date < 1939.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1940.09.01
				date < 1940.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1941.09.01
				date < 1941.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1942.09.01
				date < 1942.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1943.09.01
				date < 1943.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1944.09.01
				date < 1944.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1945.09.01
				date < 1945.09.30
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Hou zee!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event netherlands_flavour_events.11 option netherlands_flavour_events.11.a"
		name = netherlands_flavour_events.11.a
	}
}
